		<category name="Customizable Boosted Characters">
			<category name="Description">
				<comment>By Aaron0000</comment>
				<comment>Modifies the "Create New Level 30 Character" options in the save selection with a variety of options, including:</comment>
				<comment>Level - Boost the character to 50, 72, or 80 (No OP Levels yet, unfortunately.)</comment>
				<comment>Better Starting Gear - Replace the usual gear you'd get with your new character with a collection of gear more palpable than green items. Typically not the BEST gear for that character, but useful. You'll want to toggle this to match whatever level you chose for your character.</comment>
				<comment>Currencies - Set your starting values for Money, Eridium, Seraph Crystals, and Torgue Tokens.</comment>
				<comment>Playthroughs - Complete the story missions for Normal Vault Hunter Mode, or both Normal Mode and True Vault Hunter Mode to unlock Ultimate Vault Hunter Mode.</comment>
				<comment>Black Market Upgrades - Start out with a decent portion (or all) of the upgrades in the Black Market.</comment>
			</category>
			<category name="Code">
				<category name="Gunzerker">
					<category name="Player Level" MUT="true">
						<category name="50">
							<code profiles="">set GD_Level30Character.Mercenary.Profile_Mercenary30 ExpPoints 3429729</code>
						</category>
						<category name="72">
							<code profiles="">set GD_Level30Character.Mercenary.Profile_Mercenary30 ExpPoints 9520932</code>
						</category>
						<category name="80">
							<code profiles="">set GD_Level30Character.Mercenary.Profile_Mercenary30 ExpPoints 12787955</code>
						</category>
					</category>
